	#10 Anti Comitern Pact
	focus = {
		id = GER_anti_comitern_pact
		icon = GFX_goal_anti_comintern_pact
		prerequisite = { focus = GER_rhineland }
		relative_position_id = GER_rhineland
		x = -6
		y = 1
		cost = 3
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
		
		available = {
			is_puppet = no
			NOT = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = SOV
			}
			date > 1936.7.1
		}
			
		completion_reward = {
			SOV = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = pact_against_us
				}
			}
			add_named_threat = {
				threat = 1.5
				name = GER_anti_comitern_pact
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = GER
					}
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							USA = {
								NOT = {
									has_government = fascism
								}
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							tag = USA
						}
					}
					OR = {
						capital_scope = {
							is_on_continent = europe
						}
						capital_scope = {
							is_on_continent = asia
						}
						num_of_factories > 30
					}
					OR = {
						has_government = fascism
						if = {
							limit = {
								HUN = {
									fascism > 0.35
								}
							}
							tag = HUN
						}
						AND = {
							is_neighbor_of = SOV
							NOT = {
								has_government = communism
							}
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = germany.5
			}
		}
	}
